> This article is converted from Wikipedia: [아카데미 각색상](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/아카데미_각색상).


**아카데미 각색상**(Academy Award for Writing Adapted Screenplay)은 [아카데미상](../Page/아카데미상.md "wikilink") 종류의 하나로, 각색을 잘 한 작품에게 수여된다.

## 수상자와 후보자

## 각주

[각색상](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/분류:아카데미상 "wikilink") [\*](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/분류:아카데미_각색상_수상자 "wikilink") [분류:영화 각본상](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/분류:영화_각본상 "wikilink")

1.  Award entitled Best Writing, Adaptation
2.  In the 2nd and 3rd years there was only a single writing award for Writing Achievement with no distinction between original works and adaptations.
3.
4.  For the 1930/31 production year the award was again subdivided, and this one was once again Best Writing, Adaptation.
5.  Award renamed Best Writing, Screenplay
6.  Award entitled Best Screenplay—Adapted
7.  Award entitled Best Screenplay Based on Material from Another Medium
8.
9.  Though Pierre Boulle received official screen credit, it was commonly known that blacklisted writers [칼 포먼](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/칼_포먼 "wikilink") and [마이클 윌슨](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/마이클_윌슨 "wikilink") wrote the screenplay based on Boulle's novel (translated from the original French). The Board of Governors, on December 11, 1984, voted posthumous Oscars to Wilson and Foreman. It was widely reported that Boulle was surprised, as well as many others, by the nomination, especially since Boulle did not speak (or write) English.
10. Upon request of his widow and upon recommendation of the Writers Branch Executive Committee, the Board of Governors voted to restore the name of [Nedrick Young](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nedrick_Young "wikilink") to the nomination presented to [네이선 E. 더글러스](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/네이선_E._더글러스 "wikilink"), which was Young's pseudonym during the blacklisting period.
11. Originally the nomination was solely for [로버트 볼트](../Page/로버트_볼트.md "wikilink"), as Wilson was blacklisted at the time. His name was officially added to the nomination in 1995.
12. Award entitled Screenplay Adapted From Other Material
13. Award entitled Screenplay Based on Material from Another Medium
14. P.H. Vazak is a pseudonym for [로버트 타운](https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/로버트_타운 "wikilink") who was dissatisfied with the film.
15. Award entitled Best Screenplay Based on Material Previously Produced or Published
16. Award entitled Best Adapted Screenplay
